<p dir="auto"><a href="LICENSE.md"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/bbf49a2eb96e6f718803f2493bd7aa3baae61abb09b7f8fc185a94e08c504dc6/687474703a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f6c6963656e73652d4d49542d627269676874677265656e2e7376673f7374796c653d666c6174" alt="License" data-canonical-src="http://img.shields.io/badge/license-MIT-brightgreen.svg?style=flat" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://vnegi10.github.io/WeatherReport.jl/stable" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c97f0a5f2ae95755f64a27f1aa8d9a17462941fd3d6c907c7630abd5d3e60acf/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f646f63732d737461626c652d626c75652e737667" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/docs-stable-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">This package provides basic weather information right within the
terminal. Your location is not tracked, therefore, you need to specify
a city/town/village or latitude/longitude yourself. Most major locations
(population &gt; 500) around the world are supported.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-install" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>How to install?</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Press ']' to enter Pkg prompt</li>
<li>add WeatherReport</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-data-credits" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data-credits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Data credits</h2>
<p dir="auto">Weather data is obtained from <a href="https://open-meteo.com/en/docs" rel="nofollow">Open-Meteo</a> API,
which is free for non-commercial use under the Attribution 4.0 International (CC BY 4.0)
license.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-example-usage" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#example-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Example usage</h2>
<p dir="auto">For current weather conditions:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-julia notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="julia&gt; show_current(&quot;Vienna&quot;)
┌───────────────┬───────────┬────────────┬─────────────┬───────────────┬─────────┬─────────┐
│      Timezone │ Elevation │ Wind speed │ Temperature │     Condition │      🌅 │      🌆 │
│         [CET] │       [m] │     [km/h] │        [°C] │            [] │ [hh:mm] │ [hh:mm] │
├───────────────┼───────────┼────────────┼─────────────┼───────────────┼─────────┼─────────┤
│ Europe/Vienna │     196.0 │       10.1 │        11.6 │ Partly cloudy │    6:52 │   17:23 │
└───────────────┴───────────┴────────────┴─────────────┴───────────────┴─────────┴─────────┘"><pre>julia<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">show_current</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Vienna<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
┌───────────────┬───────────┬────────────┬─────────────┬───────────────┬─────────┬─────────┐
│      Timezone │ Elevation │ Wind speed │ Temperature │     Condition │      🌅 │      🌆 │
│         [CET] │       [m] │     [km<span class="pl-k">/</span>h] │        [°C] │            [] │ [hh<span class="pl-k">:</span>mm] │ [hh<span class="pl-k">:</span>mm] │

<p dir="auto">A summary of daily weather forecast can be obtained for up to a week
as shown below:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-julia notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="julia&gt; show_daily(&quot;Sofia&quot;)

<p dir="auto">To check information about your approximate location:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-julia notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="julia&gt; where_am_i()
┌──────────┬───────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────┬───────────────┬─────────────┐
│ Latitude │ Longitude │         Timezone │         City │        Region │     Country │
├──────────┼───────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼───────────────┼─────────────┤
│  51.3523 │    5.4305 │ Europe/Amsterdam │ Valkenswaard │ North Brabant │ Netherlands │
└──────────┴───────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────┴───────────────┴─────────────┘"><pre>julia<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">where_am_i</span>()
┌──────────┬───────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────┬───────────────┬─────────────┐
│ Latitude │ Longitude │         Timezone │         City │        Region │     Country │
├──────────┼───────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼───────────────┼─────────────┤
│  <span class="pl-c1">51.3523</span> │    <span class="pl-c1">5.4305</span> │ Europe<span class="pl-k">/</span>Amsterdam │ Valkenswaard │ North Brabant │ Netherlands │
└──────────┴───────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────┴───────────────┴─────────────┘</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Hourly forecast can be visualized in the REPL itself as shown in
the following examples:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-julia notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="julia&gt; plot_hourly_temp(&quot;Veldhoven&quot;)

<p dir="auto">To see a boxplot distribution of historical monthly data for a given year, use one of the
<code>plot_box_*</code> functions. For example, temperature can be visualized using <code>plot_box_temp</code>
as shown below:</p>

<p dir="auto">To compare monthly data over a given number of years, use one of the <code>compare_box_*</code>
functions. For example, temperature distribution can be visualized using
<code>compare_box_temp</code> as shown below:</p>
